na rājate sahasrāṃśuścacāla pṛthivī punaḥ  /
niṣprabhāśca grahāḥ sarve cukṣubhe ca mahodadhiḥ  // 2,37.42 //
apaśyaccānusūyātreḥ svapnaṃ bhāryā pativratā  /
kathayāmāsa viprāṇāṃ bhayādākulitekṣaṇā  // 2,37.43 //
tejasā bhāsayan kṛtsnaṃ nārāyaṇasahāyavān  /
bhikṣamāṇaḥ śivo nūnaṃ dṛṣṭo 'smākaṃ gṛheṣviti  // 2,37.44 //
tasyā vacanamākarṇya śaṅkamānā maharṣayaḥ  /
sarve jagmurmahāyogaṃ brahmāṇaṃ viśvasaṃbhavam  // 2,37.45 //
upāsyamānamamalairyogibhirbrahmavittamaiḥ  /
caturvedairmūrtimadbhiḥ sāvitryā sahitaṃ prabhum  // 2,37.46 //
āsīnamāsane ramye nānāścaryasamanvite  /
prabhāsahasrakalile jñānaiśvaryādisaṃyute  // 2,37.47 //
vibhrājamānaṃ vapuṣā sastitaṃ śubhralocanam  /
caturmukhaṃ mahābāhuṃ chandomayamajaṃ param  // 2,37.48 //
vilokya vedapuruṣaṃ prasannavadanaṃ śubham  /
śirobhirdharaṇīṃ gatvā toṣayāmāsurīśvaram  // 2,37.49 //
tān prasannamanā devaścaturmūrtiścaturmukhaḥ  /
vyājahāra muniśreṣṭhāḥ kimāgamanakāraṇam  // 2,37.50 //
tasya te vṛttamakhilaṃ brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ  /
jñāpayāñcakrire sarve kṛtvā śirasi cāñjalim  // 2,37.51 //
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kaścid dāruvanaṃ puṇyaṃ puruṣo 'tīvaśobhanaḥ  /
bhāryayā cārusarvāṅgyā praviṣṭo nagna eva hi  // 2,37.52 //
mohayāmāsa vapuṣā nārīṇāṃ kulamīśvaraḥ  /
kanyakānāṃ priyā cāsya dūṣayāmāsa putrakān  // 2,37.53 //
asmābhirvividhāḥ śāpāḥ pradattāśca parāhatāḥ  /
tāḍito 'smābhiratyarthaṃ liṅgantu vinipātitam  // 2,37.54 //
antarhitaśca bhagavān sabhāryo liṅgameva ca  /
utpātāścābhavan ghorāḥ sarvabhūtabhayaṅkarāḥ  // 2,37.55 //
ka eṣa puruṣo deva bhītāḥ sma puruṣottama  /
bhavantameva śaraṇaṃ prapannā vayamacyuta  // 2,37.56 //
tvaṃ hi vetsi jagatyasmin yatkiñcidapi ceṣṭitam  /
anugraheṇa viśveśa tadasmānanupālaya  // 2,37.57 //
vijñāpito munigaṇairviśvātmā kamalodbhavaḥ  /
dhyātvā devaṃ triśūlāṅkaṃ kṛtāñjalirabhāṣata  // 2,37.58 //
brahmovāca
hā kaṣṭaṃ bhavatāmadya jātaṃ sarvārthanāśanam  /
dhigbalaṃ dhik tapaścaryā mithyaiva bhavatāmiha  // 2,37.59 //
saṃprāpya puṇyasaṃskārānnidhīnāṃ paramaṃ nidhim  /
upekṣitaṃ vṛthācārairbhavadbhiriha mohitaiḥ  // 2,37.60 //
kāṅkṣante yogino nityaṃ yatanto yatayo nidhim  /
yameva taṃ samāsādya hā bhavadbhirupekṣitam  // 2,37.61 //
yajanti yajñairvividhairyatprāptyairvedavādinaḥ  /
mahānidhiṃ samāsādya hā bhavadbhirupekṣitam  // 2,37.62 //
yaṃ samāsādya devānaimaiśvaryamakhilaṃ jagat  /
tamāsādyākṣayanidhiṃ hā bhavadbhirupekṣitam  // 2,37.63 //
yatsamāpattijanitaṃ viśveśatvamidaṃ mama  /
tadevopekṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā nidhānaṃ bhāgyavarjitaiḥ  // 2,37.64 //
yasmin samāhitaṃ divyamaiśvaryaṃ yat tadavyayam  /
tamāsādya nidhiṃ brāhma hā bhavadbhirvṛthākṛtam  // 2,37.65 //
eṣa devo mahādevo vijñeyastu maheśvaraḥ  /
na tasya paramaṃ kiñcit padaṃ samadhigamyate  // 2,37.66 //
devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ cāpi śāśvataḥ  /
sahasrayugaparyante pralaye sarvadehinām  /
saṃharatyeṣa bhagavān kālo bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ  // 2,37.67 //
eṣa caiva prajāḥ sarvāḥ sṛjatyekaḥ svatejasā  /
eṣa cakrī ca vajrī ca śrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇaḥ  // 2,37.68 //
yogī kṛtayuge devastretāyāṃ yajña ucyate  /
dvāpare bhagavān kālo dharmaketuḥ kalau yuge  // 2,37.69 //
rudrasya mūrtayastistro yābhirviśvamidaṃ tatam  /
tamo hyagnī rajo brahmā sattvaṃ viṣṇuriti prabhuḥ  // 2,37.70 //
mūrtiranyā smṛtā cāsya digvāsā vai śivā dhruvā  /
yatra tiṣṭhati tad brahma yogena tu samanvitam  // 2,37.71 //
yā cāsya pārśvagā bhāryā bhavadbhirabhivīkṣitā  /
sā hi nārāyaṇo devaḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥ  // 2,37.72 //
tasmāt sarvamidaṃ jātaṃ tatraiva ca layaṃ vrajet  /
sa eva mohayet kṛtsnaṃ sa eva paramā gatiḥ  // 2,37.73 //
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt  /
ekaśṛṅgo mahānātmā purāṇo 'ṣṭākṣaro hariḥ  // 2,37.74 //
caturvedaścaturmūrtistrimūrtistriguṇaḥ paraḥ  /
ekamūrtirameyātmā nārāyaṇa iti śrutiḥ  // 2,37.75 //
ṛtasya garbho bhagavānāpo māyātanuḥ prabhuḥ  /
stūyate vividhairmantrairbrāhmaṇairdharmamokṣibhiḥ  // 2,37.76 //
saṃhṛtya sakalaṃ viśvaṃ kalpānte puruṣottamaḥ  /
śete yogāmṛtaṃ pītvā yat tad viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  // 2,37.77 //
na jāyate na mriyate vardhate na ca viśvasṛk  /
mūlaprakṛtiravyaktā gīyate vaidikairajaḥ  // 2,37.78 //
tato niśāyāṃ vṛttāyāṃ sisṛkṣurakhilañjagat  /
ajasya nābhau tad bījaṃ kṣipatyeṣa maheśvaraḥ  // 2,37.79 //
taṃ māṃ vitta mahātmānaṃ brahmāṇaṃ viśvato mukham  /
mahāntaṃ puruṣaṃ viśvamapāṃ garbhamanuttamam  // 2,37.80 //
na taṃ vidātha janakaṃ mohitāstasya māyayā  /
devadevaṃ mahādevaṃ bhūtānāmīśvaraṃ haram  // 2,37.81 //
eṣa devo mahādevo hyanādirbhagavān haraḥ  /
viṣṇunā saha saṃyuktaḥ karoti vikaroti ca  // 2,37.82 //
na tasya vidyate kāryaṃ na tasmād vidyate param  /
sa vedān pradadau pūrvaṃ yogamāyātanurmama  // 2,37.83 //
sa māyī māyayā sarvaṃ karoti vikaroti ca  /
tameva muktaye jñātvā vrajeta śaraṇaṃ bhavam  // 2,37.84 //
itīritā bhagavatā marīcipramukhā vibhum  /
praṇamya devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ pṛcchanti sma suduḥ khitāḥ  // 2,37.85 //
munaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ paśyema taṃ devaṃ punareva pinākinam  /
brūhi viśvāmareśāna trātā tvaṃ śaraṇaiṣiṇām  // 2,37.86 //
pitāmaha uvāca
yad dṛṣṭaṃ bhavatā tasya liṅgaṃ bhuvi nipātitam  /
talliṅgānukṛtīśasya kṛtvā liṅgamanuttamam  // 2,37.87 //
pūjayadhvaṃ sapatnīkāḥ sādaraṃ putrasaṃyutāḥ  /
vaidikaireva niyamairvividhairbrahmacāriṇaḥ  // 2,37.88 //
saṃsthāpya śāṅkarairmantrairṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃbhavaiḥ  /
tapaḥ paraṃ samāsthāya gṛṇantaḥ śatarudriyam  // 2,37.89 //
samāhitāḥ pūjayadhvaṃ saputrāḥ saha bandhubhiḥ  /
sarve prāñjalayo bhūtvā śūlapāṇiṃ prapadyatha  // 2,37.90 //
tato drakṣyatha deveśaṃ durdarśamakṛtātmabhiḥ  /
yaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvamajñānamadharmaśca praṇaśyati  // 2,37.91 //
tataḥ praṇamya varadaṃ brahmāṇamamitaujasam  /
jagmuḥ saṃhṛṣṭamanaso devadāruvanaṃ punaḥ  // 2,37.92 //
ārādhayitumārabdhā brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā  /
ajānantaḥ paraṃ devaṃ vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ  // 2,37.93 //
sthaṇḍileṣu vicitreṣu parvatānāṃ guhāsu ca  /
nadīnāṃ ca vivikteṣu pulineṣu śubheṣu ca  // 2,37.94 //
śaivālabhojanāḥ kecit kecidantarjaleśayāḥ  /
kecidabhrāvakāśāstu pādāṅguṣṭhāgraviṣṭhitāḥ  // 2,37.95 //
danto 'lūkhalinastvanye hyaśmakuṭṭāstathā pare  /
śākaparṇāśinaḥ kecit saṃprakṣālā marīcipāḥ  // 2,37.96 //
vṛkṣamūlaniketāśca śilāśayyāstathā pare  /
kālaṃ nayanti tapasā pūjayanto maheśvaram  // 2,37.97 //
tatasteṣāṃ prasādārthaṃ prapannārtiharo haraḥ  /
cakā bhagavān buddhiṃ prabodhāya vṛṣadhvajaḥ  // 2,37.98 //
devaḥ kṛtayuge hyasmin śṛṅge himavataḥ śubhe  /
devadāruvanaṃ prāptaḥ prasannaḥ parameśvaraḥ  // 2,37.99 //
bhasmapāṇḍuradigdhāṅgo nagno vikṛtalakṣaṇaḥ  /
ulmukavyagrahastaśca raktapiṅgalalocanaḥ  // 2,37.100 //
kvacicca hasate raudraṃ kvacid gāyati vismitaḥ  /
kvacinnṛtyati śṛṅgārī kvacidrauti muhurmuhuḥ  // 2,37.101 //
āśrame 'bhyāgato bhikṣāṃ yācate ca punaḥ punaḥ  /
māyāṃ kṛtvātmano rūpaṃ devastad vanamāgataḥ  // 2,37.102 //
kṛtvā girisutāṃ gaurīṃ pārśvedevaḥ pinākadhṛk  /
sā ca pūrvavad deveśī devadāruvanaṃ gatā  // 2,37.103 //
dṛṣṭvā samāgataṃ devaṃ devyā saha kapardinam  /
praṇemuḥ śirasā bhūmau toṣayāmāsurīśvaram  // 2,37.104 //
vaidikairvividhairmantraiḥ sūktairmāheśvaraiḥ śubhaiḥ  /
atharvaśirasā cānye rudrādyairbrahmabhirbhavam  // 2,37.105 //
namo devādidevāya mahādevāya te namaḥ  /
tryambakāya namastubhyaṃ triśūlavaradhāriṇe  // 2,37.106 //
namo digvāsase tubhyaṃ vikṛtāya pinākine  /
sarvapraṇatadehāya svayamapraṇatātmane  // 2,37.107 //
antakāntakṛte tubhyaṃ sarvasaṃharaṇāya ca  /
namo 'stu nṛtyaśīlāya namo bhairavarūpiṇe  // 2,37.108 //
naranārīśarīrāya yogināṃ gurave namaḥ  /
namo dāntāya śāntāya tāpasāya harāya ca  // 2,37.109 //
vibhīṣaṇāya rudrāya namaste kṛttivāsase  /
namaste lelihānāya śitikaṇṭhāya te namaḥ  // 2,37.110 //
aghoraghorarūpāya vāmadevāya vai namaḥ  /
namaḥ kanakamālāya devyāḥ priyakarāya ca  // 2,37.111 //
gaṅgāsaliladhārāya śambhave parameṣṭhine  /
namo yogādhipataye brahmādhipataye namaḥ  // 2,37.112 //
prāṇāya ca namastubhyaṃ namo bhasmāṅgarāgine  /
namaste ghanavāhāya daṃṣṭriṇe vahniretase  // 2,37.113 //
brahmaṇaśca śiro hartre namaste kālarūpiṇe  /
āgatiṃ te na janīmo gatiṃ naiva ca naiva ca  /
viśveśvara mahādeva yo 'si so 'si namo 'stu te  // 2,37.114 //
namaḥ pramathanāthāya dātre ca śubhasaṃpadām  /
kapālapāṇaye tubhyaṃ namo mīḍhuṣṭamāya te  /
namaḥ kanakaliṅgāya vāriliṅgāya te namaḥ  // 2,37.115 //
namo vahnyarkaliṅgāya jñānaliṅgāya te namaḥ  /
namo bhujaṅgahārāya karṇikārapriyāya ca  /
kirīṭine kuṇḍaline kālakālāya te namaḥ  // 2,37.116 //
vāmadeva maheśāna devadeva trilocana  /
kṣamyatāṃ yatkṛtaṃ mohāt tvameva śaraṇaṃ hi naḥ  // 2,37.117 //
caritāni vicitrāṇi guhyāni gahanāni ca  /
brahmādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ durvijñeyo 'si śaṅkara  // 2,37.118 //
ajñānād yadi vā jñānād yatkiñcitkurute naraḥ  /
tatsarvaṃ bhagavānena kurute yogamāyayā  // 2,37.119 //
evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā  /
ūcuḥ praṇamya giriśaṃ paśyāmastvāṃ yathā purā  // 2,37.120 //
teṣāṃ saṃstavamākarṇya somaḥ momavibhūṣaṇaḥ  /
svameva paramaṃ rūpaṃ darśayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ  // 2,37.121 //
taṃ te dṛṣṭvātha giriśaṃ devyā saha pinākinam  /
yathā pūrvaṃ sthitā viprāḥ praṇemurhṛṣṭamānasāḥ  // 2,37.122 //
tataste munayaḥ sarve saṃstūya ca maheśvaram  /
bhṛgvaṅgirovasiṣṭhāstu viśvāmitrastathaiva ca  // 2,37.123 //
gautamo 'triḥ sukeśaśca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ  /
marīciḥ kaśyapaścāpi saṃvartaśca mahātapāḥ  /
praṇamya devadeveśamidaṃ vacanamabruvan  // 2,37.124 //
kathaṃ tvāṃ devadeveśa karmayogena vā prabho  /
jñānena vātha yogena pūjayāmaḥ sadaiva hi  // 2,37.125 //
kena vā devamārgeṇa saṃpūjyo bhagavāniha  /
kiṃ tat sevyamasevyaṃ vā sarvametad bravīhi naḥ  // 2,37.126 //
devadeva uvāca
etad vaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi gūḍhaṃ gahanamuttamam  /
brahmaṇe kathitaṃ pūrvamādāveva maharṣayaḥ  // 2,37.127 //
sāṃkhyayogo dvidhā jñeyaḥ puruṣāṇāṃ hi sādhanam  /
yogena sahitaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ vimuktidam  // 2,37.128 //
na kevalena yogena dṛśyate puruṣaḥ paraḥ  /
jñānaṃ tu kevalaṃ samyagapavargaphalapradam  // 2,37.129 //
bhavantaḥ kevalaṃ yogaṃ samāśritya vimuktaye  /
vihāya sāṃkhyaṃ vimalamakurvanta pariśramam  // 2,37.130 //
etasmāt kāraṇād viprānṛṇāṃ kevaladharmiṇām  /
āgato 'hamimaṃ deśaṃ jñāpayan mohasaṃbhavam  // 2,37.131 //
tasmād bhavadbhirvimalaṃ jñānaṃ kaivalyasādhanam  /
jñātavyaṃ hi prayatnena śrotavyaṃ dṛśyameva ca  // 2,37.132 //
ekaḥ sarvatrago hyātmā kevalaścitimātrakaḥ  /
ānando nirmalo nityaṃ syādetat sāṃkhyadarśanam  // 2,37.133 //
etadeva paraṃ jñānameṣa mokṣo 'tra gīyate  /
etat kaivalyamamalaṃ brahmabhāvaśca varṇitaḥ  // 2,37.134 //
āśritya caitat paramaṃ tanniṣṭhāstatparāyaṇāḥ  /
paśyanti māṃ mahātmāno yatayo viśvamīśvaram  // 2,37.135 //
etat tat paramaṃ jñānaṃ kevalaṃ sannirañjanam  /
ahaṃ hi vedyo bhagavān mama mūrtiriyaṃ śivā  // 2,37.136 //
bahūni sādhanānīha siddhaye kathitāni tu  /
teṣāmabhyadhikaṃ jñānaṃ māmakaṃ dvijapuṅgavāḥ  // 2,37.137 //
jñānayogaratāḥ śāntā māmeva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  /
ye hi māṃ bhasmaniratā dhyāyanti satataṃ hṛdi  // 2,37.138 //
madbhaktiparamā nityaṃ yatayaḥ kṣīṇakalmaṣāḥ  /
nāśayāmyacirāt teṣāṃ ghoraṃ saṃsārasāgaram  // 2,37.139 //
praśāntaḥ saṃyatamanā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaḥ  /
brahmacaryarato nagno vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret  // 2,37.140 //
nirmitaṃ hi mayā pūrvaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ param  /
guhyād guhyatamaṃ sūkṣmaṃ vedasāraṃ vimuktaye  // 2,37.141 //
yad vā kaupīnavasanaḥ syād vaikavasano muniḥ  /
vedābhyāsarato vidvān dhyāyet paśupatiṃ śivam  // 2,37.142 //
eṣa pāśupato yogaḥ sevanīyo mumukṣubhiḥ  /
bhasmacchannairhi satataṃ niṣkāmairiti viśrutiḥ  // 2,37.143 //
vītarāgabhayakrodhā manmayā māmupāśritāḥ  /
bahavo 'nena yogena pūtā madbhāvamāgatāḥ  // 2,37.144 //
anyāni caiva śāstrāṇi loke 'smin mohanānitu  /
vedavādaviruddhāni mayaiva kathitāni tu  // 2,37.145 //
vāmaṃ pāśupataṃ somaṃ lākulaṃ caiva bhairavam  /
asevyametat kathitaṃ vedavāhyaṃ tathetaram  // 2,37.146 //
vedamurtirahaṃ viprā nānyaśāstrārthavedibhiḥ  /
jñāyate matsvarūpaṃ tu muktvā vedaṃ sanātanam  // 2,37.147 //
sthāpayadhvamidaṃ mārgaṃ pūjayadhvaṃ maheśvaram  /
acirādaiśvaraṃ jñānamutpatsyati na saṃśayaḥ  // 2,37.148 //
mayi bhaktiśca vipulā bhavatāmastu sattamāḥ  /
dhyātamātro hi sānnidhyaṃ dāsyāmi munisattamāḥ  // 2,37.149 //
ityuktvā bhagavān somastatraivāntaradhīyata  /
to 'pi dāruvane tasmin pūjayanti sma śaṅkaram  /
brahmacaryaratāḥ śāntā jñānayogaparāyaṇāḥ  // 2,37.150 //
sametya te mahātmāno munayo brahmavādinaḥ  /
vitenire bahūn vādānnadhyātmajñānasaṃśrayān  // 2,37.151 //
kimasya jagato mūlamātmā cāsmākameva hi  /
ko 'pi syāt sarvabhāvānāṃ heturīśvara eva ca  // 2,37.152 //
ityevaṃ manyamānānāṃ dhyānamārgāvalambinām  /
āvirāsīnmahādevī devī girivarātmajā  // 2,37.153 //
koṭisūryapratīkāśā jvālāmālāsamāvṛtā  /
svabhābhirvimalābhistu pūrayantī nabhastalam  // 2,37.154 //
tāmanvapaśyan girijāmameyāṃ
jvālāsahasrāntarasanniviṣṭām  /
praṇemurekāmakhileśapatnīṃ
jānanti te tat paramasya bījam  // 2,37.155 //
asamākameṣā parameśapatnī
gatistathātmā gaganābhidhānā  /
paśyantyathātmānamidaṃ ca kṛtsnaṃ
tasyāmathaite munayaśca viprāḥ  // 2,37.156 //
nirīkṣitāste parameśapatnyā
tadantare devamaśeṣahetum  /
paśyanti śaṃbhuṃ kavimīśitāraṃ
rudraṃ bṛhantaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam  // 2,37.157 //
ālokya devīmatha devamīśaṃ
praṇemurānandamavāpuragryam  /
jñānaṃ tadaiśaṃ bhagavatprasādā-
dāvirbabhau janmavināśahetu  // 2,37.158 //
iyaṃ hi sā jagato yonirekā
sarvātmikā sarvaniyāmikā ca  /
māheśvarīśaktiranādisiddhā
vyomābhidhānā divi rājatīva  // 2,37.159 //
asyā mahatparameṣṭhī parastā-
nmaheśvaraḥ śiva eko 'tha rudraḥ  /
cakāra viśvaṃ paraśaktiniṣṭhāṃ
māyāmathāruhya sa devadevaḥ  // 2,37.160 //
eko devaḥ sarvabhūteṣu gūḍho
māyī rudraḥ sakalo niṣkalaśca  /
sa eva devī na ca tadvibhinna-
metajjñātvā hyamṛtatvaṃ vrajanti  // 2,37.161 //
antarhito 'bhūd bhagavānatheśo
devyā bhargaḥ saha devādidevaḥ  /
ārādhayanti sma tameva devaṃ
vanaukasaste punareva rudram  // 2,37.162 //
etad vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ devadevaviceṣṭitam  /
devadāruvane pūrvaṃ purāṇe yanmayā śrutam  // 2,37.163 //
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyānnityaṃ mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  /
śrāvayed vā dvijān śāntān sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  // 2,37.164 //

iti śrīkūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryāṃ saṃhitāyāmuparivibhāge saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________


sūta uvāca
eṣā puṇyatamā devī devagandharvasevitā  /
narmadā lokavikhyātā tīrthānāmuttamā nadī  // 2,38.1 //
tasyāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ māhātmyaṃ mārkaṇḍeyena bhāṣitam  /
yudhiṣṭhirāya tu śubhaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  // 2,38.2 //
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutāstu vividhā dharmāstvatprasādānmahāmune  /
māhātmyaṃ ca prayāgasya tīrthāni vividhāni ca  // 2,38.3 //
narmadā sarvatīrthānāṃ mukhyā hi bhavateritā  /
tasyāstvidānīṃ māhātmyaṃ vaktumarhasi sattama  // 2,38.4 //
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā rudradehād viniḥ sṛtā  /
tārayet sarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca  // 2,38.5 //
narmadāyāstu māhātmyaṃ purāṇe yanmayā śrutam  /
idānīṃ tatpravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ śubham  // 2,38.6 //
puṇyā kanakhale gaṅgā kurukṣetre sarasvatī  /
grāme vā yadi vāraṇye puṇyā sarvatra narmadā  // 2,38.7 //
tribhiḥ sārasvataṃ toyaṃ saptāhena tu yāmunam  /
sadyaḥ punāti gāṅgeyaṃ darśanādeva nārmadam  // 2,38.8 //
kaliṅgadeśapaścārdhe parvate 'marakaṇṭake  /
puṇyā ca triṣu lokeṣu ramaṇīyā manoramā  // 2,38.9 //
sadevāsuragandharvā ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ  /
tapastaptvā tu rājendra siddhiṃ tu paramāṃ gatāḥ  // 2,38.10 //
tatra snātvā naro rājan niyamastho jitendriyaḥ  /
upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ kulānāṃ tārayecchatam  // 2,38.11 //
yojanānāṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ śrūyate sariduttamā  /
vistāreṇa tu rājendra yojanadvayamāyatā  // 2,38.12 //
ṣaṣṭitīrthasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭikoṭyastathaiva ca  /
parvatasya samantāt tu tiṣṭhantyamarakaṇṭake  // 2,38.13 //
brahmacārī śucirbhūtvā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ  /
sarvahiṃsānivṛttastu sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  // 2,38.14 //
evaṃ sarvasamācāro yastu prāṇān samutsṛjet  /
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ rājan śṛṇuṣvāvahito nṛpa  // 2,38.15 //
śatavarṣasahasrāṇi svarge modati pāṇḍava  /
sapsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇo divyastrīparivāritaḥ  // 2,38.16 //
divyagandhānuliptaśca divyapuṣpopaśobhitaḥ  /
krīḍate devaloke tu daivataiḥ saha modate  // 2,38.17 //
tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭo rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ  /
gṛhaṃ tu labhate 'sau vai nānāratnasamanvitam  // 2,38.18 //
stambhairmaṇimayairdivyairvajravaidūryabhūṣitam  /
ālekhyavāhanaiḥ śubhrairdāsīdāsasamanvitam  // 2,38.19 //
rājarājeśvaraḥ śrīmān sarvastrījanavallabhaḥ  /
jīved varṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ tatra bhogasamanvitaḥ  // 2,38.20 //
agnipraveśe 'tha jale athavānaśane kṛte  /
anivartikā gatistasya pavanasyāmbare yathā  // 2,38.21 //
paścime parvatataṭe sarvapāpavināśanaḥ  /
hrado jaleśvaro nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ  // 2,38.22 //
tatra piṇḍapradānena saṃdhyopāsanakarmaṇā  /
daśavarṣāṇi pitarastarpitāḥ syurna saṃśayaḥ  // 2,38.23 //
dakṣiṇe narmadākūle kapilākhyā mahānadī  /
saralārjunasaṃcchannā nātidūre vyavasthitā  // 2,38.24 //
sā tu puṇyā mahābhāgā triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā  /
tatra koṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ tīrthānāṃ tu yudhiṣṭhira  // 2,38.25 //
tasmiṃstīrthe tu ye vṛkṣāḥ patitāḥ kālaparyayāt  /
narmadātoyasaṃspṛṣṭāste yānti paramāṃ gatim  // 2,38.26 //
dvitīyā tu mahābhāgā viśalyakaraṇī śubhā  /
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā viśalyo bhavati kṣaṇāt  // 2,38.27 //
kapilā ca viśalyā ca śrūyate rājasattama  /
īśvareṇa purā proktā lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā  // 2,38.28 //
anāśakaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa  /
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,38.29 //
tatra snātvā naro rājannaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  /
ye vasantyuttare kūle rudraloke vasanti te  // 2,38.30 //
sarasvatyāṃ ca gaṅgāyāṃ narmadāyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira  /
samaṃ snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca yathā me śaṅkaro 'bravīt  // 2,38.31 //
parityajati yaḥ praṇān parvate 'marakaṇṭake  /
varṣakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,38.32 //
narmadāyāṃ jalaṃ puṇyaṃ phenormisamalaṅkṛtam  /
pavitraṃ śirasā vandya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  // 2,38.33 //
narmadā sarvataḥ puṇyā brahmahatyāpahāriṇī  /
ahorātropavāsena mucyate brahmahatyayā  // 2,38.34 //
jāleśvaraṃ tīrthavaraṃ sarvapāpavināśanam  /
tatra gatvā niyamavān sarvakāmāṃllabhennaraḥ  // 2,38.35 //
candrasūryoparāge tu gatvā hyamarakaṇṭakam  /
aśvamedhād daśaguṇaṃ puṇyamāpnoti mānavaḥ  // 2,38.36 //
eṣa puṇyo girivaro devagandharvasevitaḥ  /
nānādrumalatākīrṇo nānāpuṣpopaśobhitaḥ  // 2,38.37 //
tatra saṃnihito rājan devyā saha maheśvaraḥ  /
brahmā viṣṇustathā cendro vidyādharagaṇaiḥ saha  // 2,38.38 //
pradakṣiṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt parvataṃ hyamarakaṇṭakam  /
pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānaḥ  // 2,38.39 //
kāverī nāma vipulā nadī kalpaṣanāśinī  /
tatra snātvā mahādevamarcayed vṛṣabhadhvajam  /
saṃgame narmadāyāstu rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,38.40 //

iti śrīkūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryāṃ saṃhitāyāmuparivibhāge aṣṭātriśo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________


mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā sarvapāpavināśinī  /
munibhiḥ kathitā pūrvamīśvareṇa svayaṃbhuvā  // 2,39.1 //
munibhiḥ saṃstutā hyeṣā narmadā pravarā nadī  /
rudragātrād viniṣkrāntā lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā  // 2,39.2 //
sarvapāpaharā nityaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtā  /
saṃstutā devagandharvairapyarobhistathaiva ca  // 2,39.3 //
uttare caiva tatkūle tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam  /
nāmnā bhadreśvaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan daivataiḥ saha mohate  // 2,39.4 //
tato gaccheta rājendra tīrthamāmrātakeśvaram  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.5 //
tato 'ṅgāreśvaraṃ gacchenniyato niyatāśanaḥ  /
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,39.6 //
tato gaccheta rājendra kedāraṃ nāma puṇyadam  /
tatra snātvodakaṃ kṛtvā sarvān kāmānavāpnuyāt  // 2,39.7 //
pippaleśaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpavināśanam  /
tatra snātvā mahārāja rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,39.8 //
tato gaccheta rājendra vimaleśvaramuttamam  /
tatra prāṇān parityajya rudralokamavāpnuyāt  // 2,39.9 //
tataḥ puṣkariṇīṃ gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
snātamātro narastatra indrasyārdhāsanaṃ labhet  // 2,39.10 //
tato gaccheta rājendra śūlabhedamiti śrutam  /
tatra snātvārcayed devaṃ gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.11 //
tato gaccheta rājendra balitīrthamanuttam  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan sihāsanapatirbhavet  // 2,39.12 //
śakratīrthaṃ tato gacchet kūle caiva tu dakṣiṇe  /
upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi  // 2,39.13 //
ārādhayenmahāyogaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim  /
gosahasraphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,39.14 //
ṛṣitīrthaṃ tato gatvā sarvapāpaharaṃ nṛṇām  /
snātamātro narastatra śivaloke mahīyate  // 2,39.15 //
nāradasya tu tatraiva tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam  /
snātamātro narastatra gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.16 //
yatra taptaṃ tapaḥ pūrvaṃ nāradena surarṣiṇā  /
pratīstasya dadau yogaṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ  // 2,39.17 //
brahmaṇā nirmitaṃ liṅgaṃ brahmeśvaramiti śrutam  /
yatra snātvā naro rājan brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,39.18 //
ṛṇatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sa ṛṇānmucyate dhruvam  /
maheśvaraṃ tato gacchet paryāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam  // 2,39.19 //
bhīmeśvaraṃ tato gacchet sarvavyādhivināśanam  /
snātamātro narastatra sarvaduḥkhaiḥ pramucyate  // 2,39.20 //
tato gaccheta rājendra piṅgaleśvaramuttamam  /
ahorātropavāsena trirātraphalamāpnuyāt  // 2,39.21 //
tasmiṃmastīrthe tu rājendra kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchati  /
yāvanti tasyā romāṇi tatprasūtikuleṣu ca  /
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,39.22 //
yastu prāṇaparityāgaṃ kuryāt tatra narādhipa  /
akṣayaṃ modate kālaṃ yāvaccandradivākarau  // 2,39.23 //
narmadātaṭamāśritya tiṣṭhante ye tu mānavāḥ  /
te mṛtāḥ svargamāyānti santaḥ sukṛtino yathā  // 2,39.24 //
tato dīpteśvaraṃ gacched vyāsatīrthaṃ tapovanam  /
nivartitā purā tatra vyāsabhītā mahānadī  /
huṅkāritā tu vyāsena dakṣiṇena tato gatā  // 2,39.25 //
pradakṣiṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe yudhiṣṭhira  /
prītastasya bhaved vyāso vāñchitaṃ labhate phalam  // 2,39.26 //
tato gaccheta rājendra ikṣunadyāstu saṃgamam  /
trailokyaviśrutaṃ puṇyaṃ tatra sannihitaḥ śivaḥ  /
tatra stanātvā naro rājan gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt  // 2,39.27 //
skandatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  /
ājanmanaḥ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ snātastīvraṃ vyapohati  // 2,39.28 //
tatra devāḥ sagandharvā bhavātmajamanuttamam  /
upāsate mahātmānaṃ skandaṃ śaktidhiraṃ prabhum  // 2,39.29 //
tato gacchedāṅgirasaṃ snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
gosahasraphalaṃ prāpya rudralokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,39.30 //
aṅgirā yatra deveśaṃ brahmaputro vṛṣadhvajam  /
tapasārādhya viśveśaṃ labdhavān yogamuttamam  // 2,39.31 //
kuśatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  /
snānaṃ tatra prakurvota aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.32 //
koṭitīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  /
tatra strātvā naro rājyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ  // 2,39.33 //
candrabhāgāṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
snātamātro narastatra somaloke mahīyate  // 2,39.34 //
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle saṃgameśvaramuttamam  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.35 //
narmadāyottare kūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam  /
ādityāyatanaṃ ramyamīśvareṇa tu bhāṣitam  // 2,39.36 //
tatra snātvā tu rājendra dattvā dānaṃ tu śaktitaḥ  /
tasya tīrthaprabhāveṇa labhate cākṣayaṃ phalam  // 2,39.37 //
daridrā vyādhitā ye tu ye ca duṣkṛtakāriṇaḥ  /
mucyante sarvapāpebhyaḥ sūryalokaṃ prayānti ca  // 2,39.38 //
mārgeśvaraṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
snātamātro narastatra svargalokamavāpnuyāt  // 2,39.39 //
tataḥ paścimato gacchenmarudālayamuttamam  /
tatra snātvā tu rājendra śucirbhūtvā prayatnataḥ  // 2,39.40 //
kāñcanaṃ tu dvijo dadyād yathāvibhavavistaram  /
puṣpakeṇa vimānena vāyulokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,39.41 //
tato gaccheta rājendra ahalyātīrthamuttamam  /
snānamātrādapsarobhirmodate kālamakṣayam  // 2,39.42 //
caitramāse tu saṃprāpte śuklapakṣe trayodaśī  /
kāmadevadine tasminnahalyāṃ yastu pūjayet  // 2,39.43 //
yatra tatra narotpanno varastatra priyo bhavet  /
strīvallabho bhavecchrīmān kāmadeva ivāparaḥ  // 2,39.44 //
ayodhyāṃ tu samāsādya tīrthaṃ śakrasya viśrutam  /
snātamātro narastatra gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.45 //
somatīrthaṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
snātamātro narastatra sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  // 2,39.46 //
somagrahe tu rājendra pāpakṣayakaraṃ bhavet  /
trailokyaviśrutaṃ rājan somatīrthaṃ mahāphalam  // 2,39.47 //
yastu cāndrāyaṇaṃ kuryāt tatra tīrthe samāhitaḥ  /
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā somalokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,39.48 //
agnipraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryāt somatīrthe narādhipa  /
jale cānaśanaṃ vāpi nāsau martyo 'bhijāyate  // 2,39.49 //
stambhatīrthaṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
snātamātro narastatra somaloke mahīyate  // 2,39.50 //
tato gaccheta rājendra viṣṇutīrthamanuttamam  /
yodhanīpuramākhyātaṃ viṣṇoḥ sthānamanuttamam  // 2,39.51 //
asurā yodhitāstatra vāsudevena koṭiśaḥ  /
tatra tīrthaṃ samutpannaṃ viṣṇuśrīko bhavediha  /
ahorātropavāsena brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati  // 2,39.52 //
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam  /
kāmatīrthamiti khyātaṃ yatra kāmor'cayad bhavam  // 2,39.53 //
tasmiṃstīrthe naraḥ snātvā upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ  /
kusumāyudharūpeṇa rudroloke mahīyate  // 2,39.54 //
tato gaccheta rājendra brahmatīrthamanuttamam  /
umāhakamiti khyātaṃ tatra saṃtarpayet pitṝn  // 2,39.55 //
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ śrdhaṃ kuryād yathāvidhi  /
gajarūpā śilā tatra toyamadhye vyavasthitā  // 2,39.56 //
tasmiṃstu dāpayet piṇḍān vaiśākhyāntu viśeṣataḥ  /
snātvā samāhitamanā dambhamātsaryavarjitaḥ  /
tṛpyanti pitarastasya yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī  // 2,39.57 //
siddheśvaraṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
snātamātro narastatra gāṇapatyapadaṃ labhet  // 2,39.58 //
tato gaccheta rājendra liṅgo yatra janārdanaḥ  /
tatra snātvā tu rājendra viṣṇuloke mahīyate  // 2,39.59 //
yatra nārāyaṇo devo munonāṃ bhāvitātmanām  /
svātmānaṃ darśayāmāsa liṅgaṃ tat paramaṃ padam  // 2,39.60 //
aṅkolaṃ tu tato gacchet sarvapāpavināśanam  /
snānaṃ dānaṃ ca tatraiva brāhmaṇānāṃ ca bhojanam  /
piṇḍapridānaṃ ca kṛtaṃ pretyānantaphalapradam  // 2,39.61 //
traiyambakena toyena yaścaruṃ śrapayet tataḥ  /
aṅkolamūle dadyācca piṇḍāṃścaiva yathāvidhi  /
tāritāḥ pitarastena tṛpyantyācandratārakam  // 2,39.62 //
tato gaccheta rājendra tāpaseśvaramuttamam  /
tatra snātvā tu rājendra prāpnuyāt tapasaḥ phalam  // 2,39.63 //
śuklatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpavināśanam  /
nāsti tena sama tīrthaṃ narmadāyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira  // 2,39.64 //
darśanāt sparśanāt tasya snānadānatapojapāt  /
homāccaivopavāsācca śuklatīrthe mahat phalam  // 2,39.65 //
yojanaṃ tat smṛtaṃ kṣetraṃ devagandharvasevitam  /
śuklatīrthamiti khyātaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam  // 2,39.66 //
pādapāgreṇa dṛṣṭena brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati  /
devyā saha sadā bhargastatra tiṣṭhati śaṅkaraḥ  // 2,39.67 //
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ vaiśākhe māsi suvrata  /
kailāsāccābhiniṣkramya tatra sannihito haraḥ  // 2,39.68 //
devadānavagandharvāḥ siddhavidyādharāstathā  /
gaṇāścāpsarasāṃ nāgāstatra tiṣṭhanti puṅgava  // 2,39.69 //
rajakena yathā vastraṃ śuklaṃ bhavati vāriṇā  /
ājanmani kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śuklatīrthe vyapohati  /
snānaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ śrāddhamanantaṃ tatra dṛśyate  // 2,39.70 //
śuklatīrthāt paraṃ tīrthaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati  /
pūrve vayasi karmāṇi kṛtvā pāpāni mānavaḥ  /
ahorātropavāsena śuklatīrthe vyapohati  // 2,39.71 //
kārtikasya tu māsasya kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśī  /
ghṛtena snāpayed devamupoṣya parameśvaram  /
ekaviṃśatkulopeto na cyavedaiśvarāt padāt  // 2,39.72 //
tapasā brahmacaryeṇa yajñadānena vā punaḥ  /
na tāṃ gatimavāpnoti śuklatīrthe tu yāṃ labhet  // 2,39.73 //
śuklatīrthaṃ mahātīrthamṛṣisiddhaniṣevitam  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan punarjanma na vindati  // 2,39.74 //
ayane vā caturdaśyāṃ saṃkrāntau viṣuve tathā  /
snātvā tu sopavāsaḥ san vijitātmā samāhitaḥ  // 2,39.75 //
dānaṃ dadyād yathāśakti prīyetāṃ hariśaṅkarau  /
etat tīrthaprabhāveṇa sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam  // 2,39.76 //
anāthaṃ durgataṃ vipraṃ nāthavantamathāpi vā  /
udvādayati yastīrthe tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  // 2,39.77 //
yāvat tadromasaṃkhyā tu tatprasūtikuleṣu ca  /
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,39.78 //
tato gaccheta rājendra yamatīrtha manuttamam  /
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ māghamāse yudhiṣṭhira  /
snānaṃ kṛtvā naktabhījī na paśyed yonisaṅkaṭam  // 2,39.79 //
tato gaccheta rājendra eraṇḍītīrthamuttamam  /
saṃgame tu naraḥ snāyādupavāsaparāyaṇaḥ  /
brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayedekaṃ koṭirbhavati bhojitāḥ  // 2,39.80 //
eraṇḍīsaṃgame snātvā bhaktibhāvāt turañjitaḥ  /
mṛttikāṃ śirasi sthāpya avagāhya ca tajjalam  /
narmadodakasaṃmiśraṃ mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ  // 2,39.81 //
tato gaccheta rājendra tīrthaṃ kārṇāṭikeśvaram  /
gaṅgāvatarate tatra dine puṇye na saṃśayaḥ  // 2,39.82 //
tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca dattvā caiva yathāvidhi  /
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,39.83 //
nanditīrthaṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
prīyate tasya nandīśaḥ somaloke mahīyate  // 2,39.84 //
tato gaccheta rājendra tīrthaṃ tvanarakaṃ śubham  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan narakaṃ naiva paśyati  // 2,39.85 //
tasmiṃstīrthe tu rājendra svānyasthīni vinikṣipet  /
rūpavān jāyate loke dhanabhogasamanvitaḥ  // 2,39.86 //
tato gaccheta rājendra kapilātīrtha muttamam  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.87 //
jyeṣṭhamāse tu saṃprāpte caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ  /
tatropoṣya naro bhaktyā dadyād dīpaṃ ghṛtena tu  // 2,39.88 //
ghṛtena snāpayed rudraṃ saghṛtaṃ śrīphalaṃ dahet  /
ghaṇṭābharaṇasaṃyuktāṃ kapilāṃ vai pradāpayet  // 2,39.89 //
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ  /
śivatulyabalo bhūtvā śivavat krīḍate ciram  // 2,39.90 //
aṅgārakadine prāpte caturthyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ  /
snāpayitvā śivaṃ dadyād brāhmaṇebhyastu bhojanam  // 2,39.91 //
sarvabhogasamāyukto vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ  /
gatvā śakrasya bhavanaṃ śakreṇa saha modate  // 2,39.92 //
tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭo dhanavān bhogavān bhavet  /
aṅgārakanavamyāṃ tu amāvāsyāṃ tathaiva ca  /
snāpayet tatra yatnena rūpavān subhago bhavet  // 2,39.93 //
tato gaccheta rājendra gaṇeśvaramanuttamam  /
śrāvaṇe māsī saṃprāpte kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśī  // 2,39.94 //
snātamātro narastatra rudraloke mahīyate  /
pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā mucyate 'sāvṝṇatrayāt  // 2,39.95 //
gaṅgeśvarasamīpe tu gaṅgāvadanamuttamam  /
akāmo vā sakāmo vā tatra snātvā tu mānavaḥ  /
ājanmajanitaiḥ pāpairmucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  // 2,39.96 //
tasya vai paścime deśe samīpe nātidūrataḥ  /
daśāśvamedhikaṃ tīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam  // 2,39.97 //
upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ māsi bhādrapade śubhe  /
amāvasyāṃ naraḥ snātvā pūjayed vṛṣabhadhvajam  // 2,39.98 //
kāñcanena vimānena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā  /
gatvā rudrapuraṃ ramyaṃ rudreṇa saha modate  // 2,39.99 //
sarvatra sarvadivase snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kuryādaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.100 //

iti śrīkūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryāṃ saṃhitāyāmuparivibhāge ekonacatvāriśo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________


mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gaccheta rājendra bhṛgutīrtha manuttamam  /
tatra devo bhṛguḥ purvaṃ rudramārādhayat purā  // 2,40.1 //
darśanāt tasya devasya sadyaḥ pāpāt pramucyate  /
etat kṣetraṃ suvipulaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  // 2,40.2 //
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste 'punarbhavāḥ  /
upānahostathā yugmaṃ deyamannaṃ sakāñcanam  /
bhojanaṃ ca yathāśakti tadasyākṣayamucyate  // 2,40.3 //
kṣaranti sarvadānāni yajñadānaṃ tapaḥ kriyā  /
akṣayaṃ tat tapastaptaṃ bhṛgutīrthe yudhiṣṭhira  // 2,40.4 //
tasyaiva tapasogreṇa tuṣṭena tripurāriṇā  /
sānnidhyaṃ tatra kathitaṃ bhṛgutīrthe yudhiṣṭhira  // 2,40.5 //
tato gaccheta rājendra gautameśvaramuttamam  /
yatrārādhya triśūlāṅkaṃ gautamaḥ siddhimāpnuyāt  // 2,40.6 //
tatra snātvā naro rājan upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ  /
kāñcanena vimānena brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,40.7 //
vṛṣotsargaṃ tato gacchecchāśvataṃ padamāpnuyāt  /
na jānanti narā mūḍhā viṣṇormāyāvimohitāḥ  // 2,40.8 //
dhautapāpaṃ tato gacched dhautaṃ yatra vṛṣeṇa tu  /
narmadāyāṃ sthitaṃ rājan sarvapātakanāśanam  /
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati  // 2,40.9 //
tatra tīrthe tu rājendra prāṇatyāgaṃ karoti yaḥ  /
caturbhujastrinetraśca haratulyabalo bhavet  // 2,40.10 //
vaset kalpāyutaṃ sāgraṃ śivatulyaparākramaḥ  /
kālena mahatā jātaḥ pṛthivyāmekarāḍ bhavet  // 2,40.11 //
tato gaccheta rājendra haṃsatīrtha manuttamam  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,40.12 //
tato gaccheta rājendra siddho yatra janārdanaḥ  /
varāhatīrtha mākhyātaṃ viṣṇulokagatipradam  // 2,40.13 //
tato gaccheta rājendra candratīrthamanuttamam  /
paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣeṇa snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
snātamātro narastatra candraloke mahīyate  // 2,40.14 //
tato gaccheta rājendra kanyātīrthamanuttamam  /
śuklapakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
snātamātro narastatra pṛthivyāmekarāḍ bhavet  // 2,40.15 //
devatīrtha tato gacchet sarvadevanamakṛtam  /
tatra snātvā ca rājendra daivataiḥ saha modate  // 2,40.16 //
tato gaccheta rājendra śikhitīrthamanuttamam  /
yat tatra dīyate dānaṃ sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet  // 2,40.17 //
tato gaccheta rājendra tīrthaṃ paitāmahaṃ śubham  /
yattatra kriyate śrāddhaṃ sarvaṃ tadakṣayaṃ bhavet  // 2,40.18 //
sāvitrītīrthamāsādya yastu prāṇān parityajet  /
vidhūya sarvapāpāni brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,40.19 //
manoharaṃ tu tatraiva tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan daivataiḥ saha modate  // 2,40.20 //
tato gaccheta rājendra mānasaṃ tīrthamuttamam  /
snātvā tatra naro rājan rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,40.21 //
svargabinduṃ tato gacchettīrthaṃ devanamaskṛtam  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan durgatiṃ naiva gacchati  // 2,40.22 //
apsareśaṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret  /
krīḍate nākalokastho hyapsarobhiḥ sa modate  // 2,40.23 //
tato gaccheta rājendra bhārabhūtimanuttamam  /
upoṣitor'cayedīśaṃ rudraloke mahīyate  /
asmiṃstīrthe mṛto rājan gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt  // 2,40.24 //
kārtike māsi deveśamarcayet pārvatīpatim  /
aśvamedhād daśaguṇaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ  // 2,40.25 //
vṛṣabhaṃ yaḥ prayaccheta tatra kundendusaprabham  /
vṛṣayuktena yānena rudralokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,40.26 //
etat tīrthaṃ samāsādya yastu prāṇān parityajet  /
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,40.27 //
jalapraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa  /
haṃsayuktena yānena svargalokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,40.28 //
eraṇḍyā narmadāyāstu saṃgamaṃ lokaviśrutam  /
tatra tīrthaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  // 2,40.29 //
upavāsaparo bhūtvā nityaṃ vrataparāyaṇaḥ  /
tatra snātvā tu rājendra mucyate brahmahatyayā  // 2,40.30 //
tato gaccheta rājendra narmadodadhisaṃgamam  /
jamadagniriti khyātaḥ siddho yatra janārdanaḥ  // 2,40.31 //
tatra snātvā naro rājan narmadodadhisaṃgame  /
triguṇaṃ cāśvamedhasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ  // 2,40.32 //
tato gaccheta rājendra piṅgaleśvaramuttamam  /
tatra snātvā naro rājan rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,40.33 //
tatropavāsaṃ yaḥ kṛtvā paśyeta vimaleśvaram  /
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ hitvā yāti śivālayam  // 2,40.34 //
tato gaccheta rājendra ālikātīrthamuttamam  /
upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ niyato niyatāśanaḥ  /
asya tīrthasya māhātmyānmucyate brahmahatyayā  // 2,40.35 //
etāni tava saṃkṣepāt prādhānyāt kathitāni tu  /
na śakyā vistarād vaktuṃ saṃkhyā tīrtheṣupāṇḍava  // 2,40.36 //
eṣā pavitrā vimalā nadī trailokyaviśrutā  /
narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā mahādevasya vallabhā  // 2,40.37 //
manasā saṃsmaredyastu narmadāṃ vai yudhiṣṭhira  /
cāndrāyaṇaśataṃ sāgraṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ  // 2,40.38 //
aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣā nāstikyaṃ ghoramāśritāḥ  /
patanti narake ghore ityāha parameśvaraḥ  // 2,40.39 //
narmadāṃ sevate nityaṃ svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ  /
tena puṇyā nadī jñeyā brahmahatyāpahāriṇī  // 2,40.40 //

iti śrīkūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryāṃ saṃhitāyāmuparivibhāge catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

_____________________________________________________________


sūta uvāca
idaṃ trailokyavikhyātaṃ tīrthaṃ naimiśamuttamam  /
mahādevapriyakaraṃ mahāpātakanāśanam  // 2,41.1 //
mahādevaṃ didṛkṣūṇāmṛṣīṇaṇāṃ parameṣṭhinām  /
brahāmaṇā nirmitaṃ sthānaṃ tapastaptuṃ dvijottamāḥ  // 2,41.2 //
marīcayo 'trayo viprā vasiṣṭhāḥ kratavastathā  /
bhṛgavo 'ṅgirasaḥ pūrvā brahmāṇaṃ kamalodbhavam  // 2,41.3 //
sametya sarvavaradaṃ caturmūrti caturmukham  /
pṛcchanti praṇipatyainaṃ viśvakarmāṇamacyutam  // 2,41.4 //
ṣaṭkulīyā ūcuḥ
bhagavan devamīśānaṃ bhargamekaṃ kapardinam  /
kenopāyena paśyāmo brūhi devanamaskṛtam  // 2,41.5 //
brahmovāca
satraṃ sahasramāsadhvaṃ vāṅmanodoṣavarjitāḥ  /
deśaṃ ca vaḥ pravakṣyāmi yasmin deśe cariṣyatha  // 2,41.6 //
uktvā manomayaṃ cakraṃ sa sṛṣṭvā tānuvāca ha  /
kṣiptametanmayā cakramanuvrajata mā ciram  /
yatrāsya nemiḥ śīryeta sa deśaḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ  // 2,41.7 //
tato mumoca taccakraṃ te ca tatsamanuvrajan  /
tasya vai vrajataḥ kṣipraṃ yatra nemiraśīryata  /
naimisaṃ tatsmṛtaṃ nāmnā puṇyaṃ sarvatra pūjitam  // 2,41.8 //
siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ yakṣagandharvasevitam  /
sthānaṃ bhagavataḥ śaṃbhoretannaimiśamuttamam  // 2,41.9 //
atra devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ  /
tapastaptvā purā devā lebhire pravarān varān  // 2,41.10 //
imaṃ deśaṃ samāśritya ṣaṭkulīyāḥ samāhitāḥ  /
satreṇārādhya deveśaṃ dṛṣṭavanto maheśvaram  // 2,41.11 //
atra dānaṃ tapastaptaṃ snānaṃ japyādikaṃ ca yat  /
ekaikaṃ pāvayet pāpaṃ saptajanmakṛtaṃ dvijāḥ  // 2,41.12 //
atra pūrvaṃ sa bhagavānṛṣīṇāṃ satramāsatām  /
provāca vāyurbrahmāṇḍaṃ purāṇaṃ brahmabhāṣitam  // 2,41.13 //
atra devo mahādevo rudrāṇyā kila viśvakṛt  /
ramate 'dhyāpi bhagavān pramathaiḥ parivāritaḥ  // 2,41.14 //
atra prāṇān parityajya niyamena dvijātayaḥ  /
brahmalokaṃ gamiṣyanti yatra gatvā na jāyate  // 2,41.15 //
anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ jāpyeśvaramitiśrutam  /
jajāpa rudramaniśaṃ yatra nandī mahāgaṇaḥ  // 2,41.16 //
prītastasya mahādevo devyā saha pinākadhṛk  /
dadāvātmasamānatvaṃ mṛtyuvañcanameva ca  // 2,41.17 //
abhūdṛṣiḥ sa dharmātmā śilādo nāma dharmavit  /
ārādhayanmahādevaṃ putrārthaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam  // 2,41.18 //
tasya varṣasahasrānte tapyamānasya viśvakṛt  /
śarvaḥ somo gaṇavṛto varado 'smītyabhāṣata  // 2,41.19 //
sa vavre varamīśānaṃ vareṇyaṃ girijāpatim  /
ayonijaṃ mṛtyuhīnaṃ dehi putraṃ tvayā samam  // 2,41.20 //
tathāstvityāha bhagavān devyā saha maheśvaraḥ  /
paśyatastasya viprarṣerantardhānaṃ gato haraḥ  // 2,41.21 //
tato yiyakṣuḥ svāṃ bhūmiṃ śilādo dharmavittamaḥ  /
cakarṣa lāṅgalenorvoṃ bhittvādṛśyata śobhanaḥ  // 2,41.22 //
saṃvartakānalaprakhyaḥ kumāraḥ prahasanniva  /
rūpalāvaṇyasaṃpannastejasā bhāsayan diśaḥ  // 2,41.23 //
kumāratulyo 'pratimo meghagambhīrayā girā  /
śilādaṃ tāta tāteti prāha nandī punaḥ punaḥ  // 2,41.24 //
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nandanaṃ jātaṃ śilādaḥ pariṣasvaje  /
munibhyo darśayāmāsa ye tadāśramavāsinaḥ  // 2,41.25 //
jātakarmādikāḥ sarvāḥ kriyāstasya cakāra ha  /
upanīya yathāśāstraṃ vedamadhyāpayat sutam  // 2,41.26 //
adhītavedo bhagavān nandī matimanuttamām  /
cakre maheśvaraṃ draṣṭuṃ jeṣye mṛtyumiti prabhum  // 2,41.27 //
sa gatvā saritaṃ puṇyāmekāgraśraddhayānvitaḥ  /
jajāpa rudramaniśaṃ maheśāsaktamānasaḥ  // 2,41.28 //
tasya koṭyāṃ tu pūrṇāyāṃ śaṅkaro bhaktavatsalaḥ  /
āgatya sāmbaḥ sagaṇo varado 'smītyuvāca ha  // 2,41.29 //
sa vavre punarevāhaṃ japeyaṃ koṭimīśvaram  /
tāvadāyurmahādeva dehīti varamīśvara  // 2,41.30 //
evamastviti saṃprocya devo 'pyantaradhīyata  /
jajāpa koṭiṃ bhagavān bhūyastadgatamānasaḥ  // 2,41.31 //
dvitīyāyāṃ ca koṭyāṃ vai saṃpūrṇāyāṃ vṛṣadhvajaḥ  /
āgatya varado 'smīti prāha bhūtagaṇairvṛtaḥ  // 2,41.32 //
tṛtīyāṃ japtumicchāmi koṭiṃ bhūyo 'pi śaṅkara  /
tathāstvityāha viśvātmā devo 'pyantaradhīyata  // 2,41.33 //
koṭitraye 'tha saṃpūrṇe devaḥ prītamanā bhṛśam  /
āgatya varado 'smīti prāha bhūtagaṇairvṛtaḥ  // 2,41.34 //
japeyaṃ koṭimanyāṃ vai bhūyo 'pi tava tejasā  /
ityukte bhagavānāha na japtavyaṃ tvayā punaḥ  // 2,41.35 //
amaro jarayā tyakto mama pārśvagataḥ sadā  /
mahāgaṇapatirdevyāḥ putro bhava maheśvaraḥ  // 2,41.36 //
yogīśvaro yoganetā gaṇānāmīśvareśvaraḥ  /
sarvalokādhipaḥ śrīmān sarvajño madbalānvitaḥ  // 2,41.37 //
jñānaṃ tanmāmakaṃ divyaṃ hastāmalakavat tava  /
ābhūtasaṃplavasthāyī tato yāsyasi matpadam  // 2,41.38 //
etaduktvā mahādevo gaṇānāhūya śaṅkaraḥ  /
abhiṣekeṇa yuktena nandīśvaramayojayat  // 2,41.39 //
udvāhayāmāsa ca taṃ svayameva pinākadhṛk  /
marutāṃ ca śubhāṃ kanyāṃ suyaśeti ca viśrutām  // 2,41.40 //
etajjapyeśvaraṃ sthānaṃ devadevasya śūlinaḥ  /
yatra tatra mṛto martyo rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,41.41 //

iti śrīkūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryāṃ saṃhitāyāmuparivibhāge ekacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________


sūta uvāca
anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ japyeśvarasamīpataḥ  /
nāmnā pañcanadaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  // 2,42.1 //
trirātropoṣitastatra pūjayitvā maheśvaram  /
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,42.2 //
anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ śaṅkarasyāmitaujasaḥ  /
mahābhairavamityuktaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam  // 2,42.3 //
tīrthānāṃ ca paraṃ tīrthaṃ vitastā paramā nadī  /
sarvapāpaharā puṇyā svayameva girīndrajā  // 2,42.4 //
tīrthaṃ pañcatapaṃ nāma śaṃbhoramitatejasaḥ  /
yatra devādidevena cakrārthaṃ pūjito bhavaḥ  // 2,42.5 //
piṇḍadānādikaṃ tatra pretyānantaphalapradam  /
mṛtastatrāpi niyamād brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,42.6 //
kāyāvarohaṇaṃ nāma mahādevālayaṃ śubham  /
yatra māheśvarā dharmā munibhiḥ saṃpravartitāḥ  // 2,42.7 //
śrāddhaṃ dānaṃ tapo homa upavāsastathākṣayaḥ  /
parityajati yaḥ prāṇān rudralokaṃ sa gacchati  // 2,42.8 //
anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ kanyātīrthamiti śrutam  /
tatra gatvā tyajet prāṇāṃllokān prāpnoti śāśvatān  // 2,42.9 //
jāmadagnyasya tu śubhaṃ rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ  /
tatra snātvā tīrtha vare gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  // 2,42.10 //
mahākālamiti khyātaṃ tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam  /
gatvā prāṇān parityajya gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt  // 2,42.11 //
guhyād guhyatamaṃ tīrthaṃ nakulīśvaramuttamam  /
tatra sannihitaḥ śrīmān bhagavān nakulīśvaraḥ  // 2,42.12 //
himavacchikhare ramye gaṅgādvāre suśobhane  /
devyā saha mahādevo nityaṃ śiṣyaiśca saṃvṛtaḥ  // 2,42.13 //
tatra snātvā mahādevaṃ pūjayitvā vṛṣadhvajam  /
sarvapāpairvimucyeta mṛtastajjñānamāpnuyāt  // 2,42.14 //
anyacca devadevasya sthānaṃ puṇyatamaṃ śubham  /
bhīmeśvaramiti khyātaṃ gatvā muñcati pātakam  // 2,42.15 //
tathānyaccaṇḍavegāyāḥ saṃbhedaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ  /
tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca mucyate brahmahatyayā  // 2,42.16 //
sarveṣāmapi caiteṣāṃ tīrthānāṃ paramā purī  /
nāmnāvārāṇasī divyā koṭikoṭyayutādhikā  // 2,42.17 //
tasyāḥ purastānmāhātmyaṃ bhāṣitaṃ vo mayā tviha  /
nānyatra labhyate muktiryogināpyekajanmanā  // 2,42.18 //
ete prādhānyataḥ proktā deśāḥ pāpaharā nṛṇām  /
gatvā saṃkṣālayet pāpaṃ janmāntaraśataiḥ kṛtam  // 2,42.19 //
yaḥ svadharmān parityajya tīrthasevāṃ karoti hi  /
na tasya phalate tīrthamahi loke paratra ca  // 2,42.20 //
prāyaścittī ca vidhurastathā pāpacaro gṛhī  /
prakuryāt tīrthasaṃsevāṃ ye cānye tādṛśā janāḥ  // 2,42.21 //
sahāgnirvā sapatnīko gacchet tīrthāni yatnataḥ  /
sarvapāpavinirmukto yathoktāṃ gatimāpnuyāt  // 2,42.22 //
ṛṇāni trīṇyapākṛtya kuryād vā tīrthasevanam  /
vidhāya vṛttiṃ putrāṇāṃ bhāryāṃ teṣu nidhāya ca  // 2,42.23 //
prāyaścittaprasaṅgena tīrthamāhātmyamīritam  /
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  // 2,42.24 //

iti śrīkūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryāṃ saṃhitāyāmuparivibhāge dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________

sūta uvāca
etadākarṇya vijñānaṃ nārāyaṇamukheritam  /
kūrmarūpadharaṃ devaṃ papracchurmunayaḥ prabhum  // 2,43.1 //
munaya ūcuḥ
kathitā bhavatā dharmā mokṣajñānaṃ savistaram  /
lokānāṃ sargavistāraṃ vaṃśamanvantarāṇi ca  // 2,43.2 //
pratisargamidānīṃ no vaktumarhasī mādhava  /
bhūtānāṃ bhūtabhavyeśa yathā pūrvaṃ tvayoditam  // 2,43.3 //
sūta uvāca
śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavān kūrmarūpadhṛk  /
vyājahāra mahāyogī bhūtānāṃ pratisaṃcaram  // 2,43.4 //
kūrma uvāca
nityo naimittikaścaiva prākṛtātyantikau tathā  /
caturdhāyaṃ purāṇe 'smin procyate pratisaṃcaraḥ  // 2,43.5 //
yo 'yaṃ saṃdṛśyate nityaṃ loke bhūtakṣayastviha  /
nityaḥ saṃkīrtyate nāmnā munibhiḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ  // 2,43.6 //
brāhmo naimittiko nāma kalpānte yo bhaviṣyati  /
trailokyasyāsya kathitaḥ pratisargo manīṣibhiḥ  // 2,43.7 //
mahādādyāṃ viśeṣāntaṃ yadā saṃyāti saṃkṣayam  /
prākṛtaḥ pratisargo 'yaṃ procyate kālacintakaiḥ  // 2,43.8 //
jñānādātyantikaḥ prokto yoginaḥ paramātmani  /
pralayaḥ pratisargo 'yaṃ kālacintāparairdvijaiḥ  // 2,43.9 //
ātyantikaśca kathitaḥ pralayo 'tra sasādhanaḥ  /
naimittikamidānīṃ vaḥ kathayiṣye samāsataḥ  // 2,43.10 //
caturyugasahasrānte saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare  /
svātmasaṃsthāḥ prajāḥ kartuṃ pratipede prajāpatiḥ  // 2,43.11 //
tato bhavatyanāvṛṣṭistīvrā sā śatavārṣikī  /
bhūtakṣayakarī ghorā sarvabhūtakṣayaṅkarī  // 2,43.12 //
tato yānyalpasārāṇi sattvāni pṛthivītale  /
tāni cāgre pralīyante bhūmitvamupayānti ca  // 2,43.13 //
saptaraśmiratho bhūtvā samuttiṣṭhan divākaraḥ  /
asahyaraśmirbhavati pibannambho gabhastibhiḥ  // 2,43.14 //
tasya te raśmayaḥ sapta pibantyambu mahārṇave  /
tenāhāreṇa tā dīptāḥ sūryāḥ sapta bhavantyuta  // 2,43.15 //
tataste raśmayaḥ sapta sūryā bhūtvā caturdiśam  /
caturlokamidaṃ sarvaṃ dahanti śikhinastathā  // 2,43.16 //
vyāpnuvantaśca te viprāstūrdhvaṃ cādhaśca raśmibhiḥ  /
dīpyante bhāskarāḥ sapta yugāntāgnipratāpinaḥ  // 2,43.17 //
te sūryā vāriṇā dīptā bahusāhastraraśmayaḥ  /
khaṃ samāvṛtya tiṣṭhanti nirdahanto vasuṃdharām  // 2,43.18 //
tatasteṣāṃ pratāpena dahyamānā vasuṃdharā  /
sādrinadyarṇavadvīpā nisnehā samapadyata  // 2,43.19 //
dīptābhiḥ saṃtatābhiśca raśmibhirvai samantataḥ  /
adhaścordhvaṃ ca lagnābhistiryak caiva samāvṛtam  // 2,43.20 //
sūryāgninā pramṛṣṭānāṃ saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ parasparam  /
ekatvamupayātānāmekajvālaṃ bhavatyuta  // 2,43.21 //
sarvalokapraṇāśaśca so 'gnirbhūtvā sukuṇḍalī  /
caturlokamidaṃ sarvaṃ nirdahatyātmatejasā  // 2,43.22 //
tataḥ pralīne sarvasmiñ jaṅgame sthāvare tathā  /
nirvṛkṣā nistṛṇā bhūmiḥ kūrmapṛṣṭhā prakāśate  // 2,43.23 //
ambarīṣamivābhāti sarvamāpūritaṃ jagat  /
sarvameva tadarcirbhiḥ pūrṇaṃ jājvalyate punaḥ  // 2,43.24 //
pātāle yāni sattvāni mahodadhigatāni ca  /
tatastāni pralīyante bhūmitvamupayānti ca  // 2,43.25 //
dvīpāṃśca parvatāṃścaiva varṣāṇyatha mahodadhīn  /
tān sarvān bhasmasāt kṛtvā saptātmā pāvakaḥ prabhuḥ  // 2,43.26 //
samudrebhyo nadībhyaśca pātālebhyaśca sarvaśaḥ  /
pibannapaḥ samiddho 'gniḥ pṛthivīmāśrito jvalan  // 2,43.27 //
tataḥ saṃvartakaḥ śailānatikramya mahāṃstathā  /
lokān dahati dīptātmā rudratejovijṝmbhitaḥ  // 2,43.28 //
sa dagdhvā pṛthivīṃ devo rasātalamaśoṣayat  /
adhastāt pṛthivīṃ dagdhvā divamūrdhvaṃ dahiṣyati  // 2,43.29 //
yojanānāṃ śatānīha sahasrāṇyayutāni ca  /
uttiṣṭhanti śikhāstasya vahneḥ saṃvartakasya tu  // 2,43.30 //
gandharvāṃśca piśācāṃśca sayakṣoragarākṣasān  /
tadā dahatyasau dīptaḥ kālarudrapracoditaḥ  // 2,43.31 //
bhūrlokaṃ ca bhuvarlokaṃ svarlokaṃ ca tathā mahaḥ  /
dahedaśeṣaṃ kālāgniḥ kālo viśvatanuḥ svayam  // 2,43.32 //
vyāpteṣveteṣu lokeṣu tiryagūrdhvamathāgninā  /
tat tejaḥ samanuprāpya kṛtsnaṃ jagadidaṃ śanaiḥ  /
ayoguḍanibhaṃ sarvaṃ tadā caikaṃ prakāśate  // 2,43.33 //
tato gajakulonnādāstaḍidbhiḥ samalaṅkṛtāḥ  /
uttiṣṭhanti tadā vyomni ghorāḥ saṃvartakā ghanāḥ  // 2,43.34 //
kecinnīlotpalaśyāmāḥ kecit kumudasannibhāḥ  /
dhūmravarṇāstathā kecit kecit pītāḥ payodharāḥ  // 2,43.35 //
kecid rāsabhavarṇāstu lākṣārasanibhāstathā  /
śaṅkhakundanibhāścānye jātyañjananibhāḥ pare  // 2,43.36 //
manaḥ śilābhāstvanye ca kapotasadṛśāḥ pare  /
indragopanibhāḥ keciddharitālanibhāstathā  /
indracāpanibhāḥ keciduttiṣṭhanti ghanā divi  // 2,43.37 //
kecit parvatasaṃkāśāḥ kecid gajakulopamāḥ  /
kūṭāṅgāranibhāścānye kecinmīnakulodvahāḥ  /
bahūrūpā ghorūpā ghorasvaraninādinaḥ  // 2,43.38 //
tadā jaladharāḥ sarve pūrayanti nabhaḥ sthalam  /
tataste jaladā ghorā rāviṇo bhāskarātmajāḥ  /
saptadhā saṃvṛtātmānastamagniṃ śamayantyuta  // 2,43.39 //
tataste jaladā varṣaṃ muñcantīha mahaughavat  /
sughoramaśivaṃ sarvaṃ nāśayanti ca pāvakam  // 2,43.40 //
pravṛṣṭe ca tadātyarthamambhasā pūryate jagat  /
adbhistejobhibhūtatvāt tadāgniḥ praviśatyapaḥ  // 2,43.41 //
naṣṭe cāgnau varṣaśataiḥ payodāḥ kṣayasaṃbhavāḥ  /
plāvayanto 'tha bhuvanaṃ mahājalaparistravaiḥ  // 2,43.42 //
dhārābhiḥ pūrayantīdaṃ codyamānāḥ svayaṃbhuvā  /
atyantasalilaughaiśca velā iva mahodadhiḥ  // 2,43.43 //
sādridvīpā tathā pṛthvī jalaiḥ saṃcchādyate śanaiḥ  /
ādityaraśmibhiḥ pītaṃ jalamabhreṣu tiṣṭhati  /
punaḥ patati tad bhūmau pūryante tena cārṇavāḥ  // 2,43.44 //
tataḥ samudrāḥ svāṃ velāmatikrāntāstu kṛtsnaśaḥ  /
parvatāśca vilīyante mahī cāpsu nimajjati  // 2,43.45 //
tasminnekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame  /
yoganindrāṃ samāsthāya śete devaḥ prajāpatiḥ  // 2,43.46 //
caturyugasahasrāntaṃ kalpamāhurmaharṣayaḥ  /
vārāho vartate kalpo yasya vistāra īritaḥ  // 2,43.47 //
asaṃkhyātāstathā kalpā brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakāḥ  /
kathitā hi purāṇeṣu munibhiḥ kālacintakaiḥ  // 2,43.48 //
sāttvikeṣvatha kalpeṣu māhātmyamadhikaṃ hareḥ  /
tāmaseṣu harasyoktaṃ rājaseṣu prajāpateḥ  // 2,43.49 //
yo 'yaṃ pravartate kalpo vārāhaḥ sāttviko mataḥ  /
anye ca sāttvikāḥ kalpā mama teṣu parigrahaḥ  // 2,43.50 //
dhyānaṃ tapastathā jñānaṃ labdhvā teṣveva yoginaḥ  /
ārādhya giriśaṃ māṃ ca yānti tat paramaṃ padam  // 2,43.51 //
so 'haṃ sattvaṃ samāsthāya māyī māyāmayīṃ svayam  /
ekārṇave jagatyasmin yoganidrāṃ vrajāmi tu  // 2,43.52 //
māṃ paśyanti mahātmānaḥ suptaṃ kālaṃ maharṣayaḥ  /
janaloke vartamānāstapasā yogacakṣuṣā  // 2,43.53 //
ahaṃ purāṇapuruṣo bhūrbhuvaḥ prabhavo vibhuḥ  /
sahasracaraṇaḥ śrīmān sahasrāṃśuḥ sahasradṛk  // 2,43.54 //
mantro 'gnirbrāhmiṇā gāvaḥ kuśāśca samidho hyaham  /
prokṣaṇī ca śruvaścaiva somo ghṛtamathāsmyaham  // 2,43.55 //
saṃvartako mahānātmā pavitraṃ paramaṃ yaśaḥ  /
vedo vedyaṃ prabhurgoptā gopatirbrahmaṇo mukham  // 2,43.56 //
anantastārako yogī gatirgatimatāṃ varaḥ  /
haṃsaḥ prāṇo 'tha kapilo viśvamūrtiḥ sanātanaḥ  // 2,43.57 //
kṣetrajñaḥ prakṛtiḥ kālo jagadbījamathāmṛtam  /
mātā pitā mahādevo matto hyanyanna vidyate  // 2,43.58 //
ādityavarṇo bhuvanasya goptā
nārāyaṇaḥ puruṣo yogamūrtiḥ  /
māṃ paśyanti yatayo yoganiṣṭhā
jñātvātmānamamṛtatvaṃ vrajanti  // 2,43.59 //

iti śrīkūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryāṃ saṃhitāyāmuparivibhāge tricatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________


kūrma uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi pratisargamanuttamam  /
prākṛtaṃ hi samāsena śṛṇudhvaṃ gadato mama  // 2,44.1 //
gate parārdhadvitaye kālo lokaprakālanaḥ  /
kālāgnirbhasmasāt kartuṃ karoti nikilaṃ matim  // 2,44.2 //
svātmanyātmānamāveśya bhūtvā devo maheśvaraḥ  /
dahedaśeṣaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam  // 2,44.3 //
tamāviśya mahādevo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ  /
karoti lokasaṃhāraṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ rūpamāśritaḥ  // 2,44.4 //
praviśya maṇḍalaṃ sauraṃ kṛtvāsau bahudhā punaḥ  /
nirdahatyakhilaṃ lokaṃ saptasaptisvarūpadhṛk  // 2,44.5 //
sa dagdhvā sakalaṃ sattvamastraṃ brahmaśiro mahat  /
devatānāṃ śarīreṣu kṣipatyakhiladāhakam  // 2,44.6 //
dagdheṣvaśeṣadeveṣu devī girivarātmajā  /
ekāsā sākṣiṇī śaṃbhostiṣṭhate vaidikī śrutiḥ  // 2,44.7 //
śiraḥ kapālairdevānāṃ kṛtastragvarabhūṣaṇaḥ  /
ādityacandrādigaṇaiḥ pūrayan vyomamaṇḍalam  // 2,44.8 //
sahasranayano devaḥ sahasrākṛtiriśvaraḥ  /
sahasrahastacaraṇaḥ sahasrārcirmahābhujaḥ  // 2,44.9 //
daṃṣṭrākarālavadanaḥ pradīptānalalocanaḥ  /
triśūlī kṛttivasano yogamaiśvaramāsthitaḥ  // 2,44.10 //
pītvā tatparamānandaṃ prabhūtamamṛtaṃ svayam  /
karoti tāṇḍavaṃ devīmālokya parameśvaraḥ  // 2,44.11 //
pītvā nṛttāmṛtaṃ devī bhartuḥ paramamaṅgalā  /
yogamāsthāya devasya dehamāyāti śūlinaḥ  // 2,44.12 //
saṃtyaktvā tāṇḍavarasaṃ svecchayaiva pinākadhṛk  /
jyotiḥ svabhāvaṃ bhagavān dagdhvā brahmāṇḍamaṇḍalam  // 2,44.13 //
saṃsthiteṣvatha deveṣu brahmaviṣṇupinākiṣu  /
guṇairaśeṣaiḥ pṛthivīvilayaṃ yāti vāriṣu  // 2,44.14 //
sa vāritattvaṃ saguṇaṃ grasate havyavāhanaḥ  /
tejastu guṇasaṃyuktaṃ vāyau saṃyāti saṃkṣayam  // 2,44.15 //
ākāśe saguṇo vāyuḥ pralayaṃ yāti viśvabhṛt  /
bhūtādau ca tathākāśaṃ līyate guṇasaṃyutam  // 2,44.16 //
indriyāṇi ca sarvāṇi taijase yānti saṃkṣayam  /
vaikārike devagaṇāḥ pralaṃya yānti sattamāḥ  // 2,44.17 //
vaikārikastaijasaśca bhūtādiśceti sattamāḥ  /
trividho 'yamahaṅkāro mahati pralaṃya vrajet  // 2,44.18 //
mahāntamebhiḥ sahitaṃ brahmāṇamatitejasam  /
avyaktaṃ jagato yoniḥ saṃharedekamavyayam  // 2,44.19 //
evaṃ saṃhṛtya bhūtāni tattvāni ca maheśvaraḥ  /
viyojayati cānyonyaṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ param  // 2,44.20 //
pradhānapuṃsorajayoreṣa saṃhāra īritaḥ  /
maheśvarecchājanito na svayaṃ vidyate layaḥ  // 2,44.21 //
guṇasāmyaṃ tadavyaktaṃ prakṛtiḥ parigīyate  /
pradhānaṃ jagato yonirmāyātattvamacetanam  // 2,44.22 //
kūṭasthaścinmayo hyātmā kevalaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ  /
gīyate munibhiḥ sākṣī mahānekaḥ pitāmahaḥ  // 2,44.23 //
evaṃ saṃhārakaraṇī śaktirmāheśvarī dhruvā  /
pradhānādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ dahed rudra iti śrutiḥ  // 2,44.24 //
yogināmatha sarveṣāṃ jñānavinyastacetasām  /
ātyantikaṃ caiva layaṃ vidadhātīha śaṅkaraḥ  // 2,44.25 //
ityeṣa bhagavān rudraḥ saṃhāraṃ kurute vaśī  /
sthāpikā mohanī śaktirnārāyaṇa iti śrutiḥ  // 2,44.26 //
hiraṇyagarbhā bhagavān jagat sadasadātmakam  /
sṛjedaśeṣaṃ prakṛtestanmayaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ  // 2,44.27 //
sarvajñāḥ sarvagāḥ śāntāḥ svātmanyevavyavasthitāḥ  /
śaktayo brahmaviṇvīśā bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ  // 2,44.28 //
sarveśvarāḥ sarvavandyāḥ śāśvatānantabhoginaḥ  /
ekamevākṣaraṃ tattvaṃ puṃpradhāneśvarātmakam  // 2,44.29 //
anyāśca śaktayo divyāḥ santi tatra sahasraśaḥ  /
ijyante vividhairyajñaiḥ śakrādityādayo 'marāḥ  // 2,44.30 //
ekaikasya sahasrāṇi dehānāṃ vai śatāni ca  /
kathyante caiva māhātmyācchaktirekaiva nirguṇāḥ  // 2,44.31 //
tāṃ tāṃ śaktiṃ samādhāya svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ  /
karoti dehān vividhān grasate caiva līlayā  // 2,44.32 //
ijyate sarvayajñeṣu brāhmaṇairvedavādibhiḥ  /
sarvakāmaprado rudra ityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ  // 2,44.33 //
sarvāsāmeva śaktīnāṃ brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ  /
prādhānyena smṛtā devāḥ śaktayaḥ paramātmanaḥ  // 2,44.34 //
ādyaḥ parastād bhagavān paramātmā sanātanaḥ  /
gīyate sarvaśaktyātmā śūlapāṇirmaheśvaraḥ  // 2,44.35 //
enameke vadantyagniṃ nārāyaṇamathāpare  /
indrameke pare viśvān brahmāṇamapare jaguḥ  // 2,44.36 //
brahmaviṣṇavagnivaruṇāḥ sarve devāstatharṣayaḥ  /
ekasyaivātha rudrasya bhedāste parikīrtitāḥ  // 2,44.37 //
yaṃ yaṃ bhedaṃ samāśritya yajanti parameśvaram  /
tat tad rūpaṃ samāsthāya pradadāti phalaṃ śivaḥ  // 2,44.38 //
tasmādekataraṃ bhedaṃ samāśrityāpi śāśvatam  /
ārādhayanmahādevaṃ yāti tatparamaṃ padam  // 2,44.39 //
kintu devaṃ mahādevaṃ sarvaśaktiṃ sanātanam  /
ārādhayed vai giriśaṃ saguṇaṃ vātha nirguṇam  // 2,44.40 //
mayā prokto hi bhavatāṃ yogaḥ prāgeva nirguṇaḥ  /
ārurukṣustu saguṇaṃ pūjayet parameśvaram  // 2,44.41 //
pinākinaṃ trinayanaṃ jaṭilaṃ kṛttivāsasam  /
padmāsanasthaṃ rukmābhaṃ cintayed vaidikī śrutiḥ  // 2,44.42 //
eṣa yogaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ sabījo munisattamāḥ  /
tasmāt sarvān parityajya devān brahmapurogamān  /
ārādhayed virūpākṣamādimadhyāntasaṃsthitam  // 2,44.43 //
bhaktiyogasamāyuktaḥ svadharmanirataḥ śuciḥ  /
tādṛśaṃ rūpamāsthāya samāyātyantikaṃ śivam  // 2,44.44 //
eṣa yogaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ sabījo 'tyantabhāvane  /
yathāvidhi prakurvāṇaḥ prāpnuyādaiśvaraṃ padam  // 2,44.45 //
atrāpyaśakto 'tha haraṃ viṣṇuṃ bahmāṇamarcayet  /
atha cedasamarthaḥ syāt tatrāpi munipuṅgavāḥ  /
tato vāyvagniśakrādīn pūjayed bhaktisaṃyutaḥ  // 2,44.46 //
ye cānye bhāvane śuddhe prāgukte bhavatāmiha  /
athāpi kathito yogo nirbojaśca sabījakaḥ  // 2,44.47 //
jñānaṃ taduktaṃ nirbojaṃ pūrvaṃ hi bhavatāṃ mayā  /
viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ virañciṃ ca sabījaṃ bhāvayed budhaḥ  /
sathavāgnyādikān devāṃstatparaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ  // 2,44.48 //
pūjayet puruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ caturmūrtidharaṃ harim  /
anādinidhanaṃ devaṃ vāsudevaṃ sanātanam  // 2,44.49 //
nārāyaṇaṃ jagadyonimākāśaṃ paramaṃ padam  /
talliṅgadhārī niyataṃ tadbhaktastadapāśrayaḥ  /
eṣa eva vidhirbrāhme bhāvane cāntike mataḥ  // 2,44.50 //
ityetat kathitaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvanāsaṃśrayaṃ param  /
indradyumnāya munaye kathitaṃ yanmayā purā  // 2,44.51 //
avyaktātmakamevedaṃ cetanācetanaṃ jagat  /
tadīśvaraḥ paraṃ brahma tasmād brahmamayaṃ jagat  // 2,44.52 //
sūta uvāca
etāvaduktvā bhagavān virarāma janārdanaḥ  /
tuṣṭuvurmunayo viṣṇuṃ śakreṇa saha mādhavam  // 2,44.53 //
munaya ūcuḥ
namaste kūrmarūpāya viṣṇave paramātmane  /
nārāyaṇāya viśvāya vāsudevāya te namaḥ  // 2,44.54 //
namo namaste kṛṣṇāya govindāya namo namaḥ  /
mādhavāya namastubhyaṃ namo yajñeśvarāya ca  // 2,44.55 //
sahasraśirase tubhyaṃ sahasrākṣāya te namaḥ  /
namaḥ sahasrahastāya sahasracaraṇāya ca  // 2,44.56 //
oṃ namo jñānarūpāya paramātmasvarūpiṇe  /
ānandāya namastubhyaṃ māyātītāya te namaḥ  // 2,44.57 //
namo gūḍhaśarīrāya nirguṇāya namo 'stu te  /
puruṣāya purāṇāya sattāmātrasvarūpiṇe  // 2,44.58 //
namaḥ sāṃkhyāya yogāya kevalāya namo 'stu te  /
dharmajñānādhigamyāya niṣkalāya namo namaḥ  // 2,44.59 //
namostu vyomatattvāya mahāyogeśvarāya ca  /
parāvarāṇāṃ prabhave vedavedyāya te namaḥ  // 2,44.60 //
namo buddhāya śuddhāya namo yuktāya hetave  /
namo namo namastubhyaṃ māyine vedhase namaḥ  // 2,44.61 //
namo 'stu te varāhāya nārasiṃhāya te namaḥ  /
vāmanāya namastubhyaṃ hṛṣīkeśāya te namaḥ  // 2,44.62 //
namo 'stu kālarudrāya kālarūpāya te namaḥ  /
svargāpavargadātre ca namo 'pratihatātmane  // 2,44.63 //
namo yogādhigamyāya yogine yogadāyine  /
devānāṃ pataye tubhyaṃ devārtiśamanāya te  // 2,44.64 //
bhagavaṃstvatprasādena sarvasaṃsāranāśanam  /
asmābhirviditaṃ jñānaṃ yajjñātvāmṛtamaśnute  // 2,44.65 //
śrutāstu vividhā dharmā vaṃśā manvantarāṇi ca  /
sargaśca pratisargaśca brahmāṇyasyāsya vistaraḥ  // 2,44.66 //
tvaṃ hi sarvajagatsākṣī viśvo nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ  /
trātumarhasyanantātmaṃstvameva śaraṇaṃ gatiḥ  // 2,44.67 //
sūta uvāca
etad vaḥ kathitaṃ viprā yogamokṣapradāyakam  /
kaurmaṃ purāṇamakhilaṃ yajjagāda gadādharaḥ  // 2,44.68 //
asmin purāṇe lakṣmyāstu saṃbhavaḥ kathitaḥ purā  /
mohāyāśeṣabhūtānāṃ vāsudevena yojanam  // 2,44.69 //
prajāpatīnāṃ sargastu varṇadharmāśca vṛttayaḥ  /
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ yathāvallakṣaṇaṃ śubham  // 2,44.70 //
pitāmahasya viṣṇośca maheśasya ca dhīmataḥ  /
ekatvaṃ ca pṛthaktvaṃ ca viśeṣaścopavarṇitaḥ  // 2,44.71 //
bhaktānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ samācāraśca śobhanaḥ  /
varṇāśramāṇāṃ kathitaṃ yathāvadiha lakṣaṇam  // 2,44.72 //
ādisargastataḥ paścādaṇḍāvaraṇasaptakam  /
hiraṇyagarbhasargaśca kīrtito munipuṅgavāḥ  // 2,44.73 //
kālasaṃkhyāprakathanaṃ māhātmyaṃ ceśvarasya ca  /
brahmaṇaḥ śayanaṃ cāpsu nāmanirvacanaṃ tathā  // 2,44.74 //
varāhavapuṣā bhūyo bhūmeruddharaṇaṃ punaḥ  /
mukhyādisargakathanaṃ munisargastathāparaḥ  // 2,44.75 //
vyākhyato rudrasargaśca ṛṣisargaśca tāpasaḥ  /
dharmasya ca prajāsargastāmasāt pūrvameva tu  // 2,44.76 //
brahmaviṣṇuvivādaḥ syādantardehapraveśanam  /
padmodbhavatvaṃ devasya mohastasya ca dhīmataḥ  // 2,44.77 //
darśanaṃ ca maheśasya māhātmyaṃ viṣṇuneritam  /
divyadṛṣṭipradānaṃ ca brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  // 2,44.78 //
saṃstavo devadevasya brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā  /
prasādo giriśasyātha varadānaṃ tathaiva ca  // 2,44.79 //
saṃvādo viṣṇunā sārdhaṃ śaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ  /
varadānaṃ tathāpūrvamantardhānaṃ pinākinaḥ  // 2,44.80 //
vadhaśca kathito viprā madhukaiṭabhayoḥ purā  /
avatāro 'tha devasya brahmaṇo nābhipaṅkajāt  // 2,44.81 //
ekībhāvaśca devasya viṣṇunā kathitastataḥ  /
vimoho brahmaṇaścātha saṃjñālābho harestataḥ  // 2,44.82 //
tapaścaraṇamākhyātaṃ devadevasya dhīmataḥ  /
prādurbhāvo maheśasya lalāṭāt kathitastataḥ  // 2,44.83 //
rudrāṇāṃ kathitā sṛṣṭirbrahmaṇaḥ pratiṣedhanam  /
bhūtiśca devadevasya varadānopadeśakau  // 2,44.84 //
antardhānaṃ ca rudrasya tapaścaryāṇḍajasya ca  /
darśanaṃ devadevasya naranārīśarīratā  // 2,44.85 //
devyā vibhāgakathanaṃ devadevāt pinākinaḥ  /
devyāstu paścāt kathitaṃ dakṣaputrītvameva ca  // 2,44.86 //
himavadduhitṛtvaṃ ca devyā māhātmyameva ca  /
darśanaṃ divyarūpasya vaiśvarūpasya darśanam  // 2,44.87 //
nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ kathitaṃ pitrā himavatā svayam  /
upadeśo mahādevyā varadānaṃ tathaiva ca  // 2,44.88 //
bhṛgvādīnāṃ prajāsargo rājñāṃ vaṃśasya vistaraḥ  /
prācetasatvaṃ dakṣasya dakṣayajñavimardanam  // 2,44.89 //
dadhīcasya ca dakṣasya vivādaḥ kathitastadā  /
tataśca śāpaḥ kathito munīnāṃ munipuṅgavāḥ  // 2,44.90 //
rudrāgatiḥ prasādaśca antardhānaṃ pinākinaḥ  /
pitāmahasyopadeśaḥ kīrtyate rakṣaṇāya tu  // 2,44.91 //
dakṣasya ca prajāsargaḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ  /
hiraṇyakaśipornāśo hiraṇyākṣavadhastathā  // 2,44.92 //
tataśca śāpaḥ kathito devadāruvanaukasām  /
nigrahaścāndhakasyātha gāṇapatyamanuttamam  // 2,44.93 //
prahrādanigrahaścātha baleḥ saṃyamanaṃ tataḥ  /
bāṇasya nigrahaścātha prasādastasya śūlinaḥ  // 2,44.94 //
ṛṣīṇāṃ vaṃśavistāro rājñāṃ vaṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  /
vasudevāt tato viṣṇorutpattiḥ svecchayā hareḥ  // 2,44.95 //
darśanaṃ copamanyorvai tapaścaraṇameva ca  /
varalābho mahādevaṃ dṛṣṭvā sāmbaṃ trilocanam  // 2,44.96 //
kailāsagamanaṃ cātha nivāsastatra śārṅgiṇaḥ  /
tataśca kathyate bhītirdvārivatyā nivāsinām  // 2,44.97 //
rakṣaṇaṃ garuḍenātha jitvā śatrūn mahābalān  /
nārādāgamanaṃ caiva yātrā caiva garutmataḥ  // 2,44.98 //
tataśca kṛṣṇāgamanaṃ munīnāmāgatistataḥ  /
naityakaṃ vāsudevasya śivaliṅgārcanaṃ tathā  // 2,44.99 //
mārkaṇḍeyasya ca muneḥ praśnaḥ proktastataḥ param  /
liṅgārcananimittaṃ ca liṅgasyāpi saliṅginaḥ  // 2,44.100 //
yathātmyakathanaṃ cātha liṅgāvirbhāva eva ca  /
brahmaviṣṇostathā madhye kīrtito munipuṅgavāḥ  // 2,44.101 //
mohastayostu kathito gamanaṃ cordhvato 'pyadhaḥ  /
saṃstavo devadevasya prasādaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  // 2,44.102 //
antardhānaṃ ca liṅgasya sāmbotpattistataḥ param  /
kīrtitā cāniruddhasya samutpattirdvijottamāḥ  // 2,44.103 //
kṛṣṇasya gamane buddhirṛṣīṇāmāgatistathā  /
anuvaśāsitaṃ ca kṛṣṇena varadānaṃ mahātmanaḥ  // 2,44.104 //
gamanaṃ caiva kṛṣṇasya pārthasyāpi ca darśanam  /
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasyoktā yugadharmāḥ sanātanāḥ  // 2,44.105 //
anugraho 'tha pārthasya vārāṇasīgatistataḥ  /
pārāśaryasya ca munervyāsasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ  // 2,44.106 //
vāraṇasyāśca māhātmyaṃ tīrthānāṃ caiva varṇanam  /
tīrthayātrā ca vyāsasya devyāścaivātha darśanam  /
udvāsanaṃ ca kathitaṃ varadānaṃ tathaiva ca  // 2,44.107 //
prayāgasya ca māhātmyaṃ kṣetrāṇāmatha kīrtinam  /
phalaṃ ca vipulaṃ viprā mārkaṇḍeyasya nirgamaḥ  // 2,44.108 //
bhuvanānāṃ svarūpaṃ ca jyotiṣāṃ ca niveśanam  /
kīrtyante caiva varṣāṇi nadīnāṃ caiva nirṇayaḥ  // 2,44.109 //
parvatānāṃ ca kathanaṃ sthānāni ca divaukasām  /
dvīpānāṃ pravibhāgaśca śvetadvīpopavarṇanam  // 2,44.110 //
śayanaṃ keśavasyātha māhātmyaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ  /
manvantarāṇāṃ kathanaṃ viṣṇormāhātmyameva ca  // 2,44.111 //
vedaśākhāpraṇayanaṃ vyāsānāṃ kathanaṃ tataḥ  /
avedasya ca vedānāṃ kathanaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ  // 2,44.112 //
yogeśvarāṇāṃ ca kathā śiṣyāṇāṃ cātha kīrtanam  /
gītāśca vividhāguhyā īśvarasyātha kīrtitāḥ  // 2,44.113 //
varṇāśramāṇāmācārāḥ prāyaścittavidhistataḥ  /
kapālitvaṃ ca rudrasya bhikṣācaraṇameva ca  // 2,44.114 //
pativratāyāścākhyānaṃ tīrthānāṃ ca vinirṇayaḥ  /
tathā maṅkaṇakasyātha nigrahaḥ kīrtyate dvijāḥ  // 2,44.115 //
vadhaśca kathito viprāḥ kālasya ca samāsataḥ  /
devadāruvane śaṃbhoḥ praveśo mādhavasya ca  // 2,44.116 //
darśanaṃ ṣaṭkulīyānāṃ devadevasya dhīmataḥ  /
varadānaṃ ca devasya nandine tu prakīrtitam  // 2,44.117 //
naimittikastu kathitaḥ pratisargastataḥ param  /
prākṛtaḥ pralayaścordhvaṃ sabījo yoga eva ca  // 2,44.118 //
evaṃ jñātvā purāṇasya saṃkṣepaṃ kīrtayet tu yaḥ  /
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,44.119 //
evamuktvā śriyaṃ devīmādāya puruṣottamaḥ  /
saṃtyajya kūrmasaṃsthānaṃ svasthānaṃ ca jagāma ha  // 2,44.120 //
devāśca sarve munayaḥ svāni sthānāni bhejire  /
praṇamya puruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ gṛhītvā hyamṛtaṃ dvijāḥ  // 2,44.121 //
etat purāṇaṃ paramaṃ bhāṣitaṃ kūrmarūpiṇā  /
sākṣād devādidenena viṣṇunā viśvayoninā  // 2,44.122 //
yaḥ paṭhet satataṃ martyo niyamena samāhitaḥ  /
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,44.123 //
likhitvā caiva yo dadyād vaiśākhe māsi suvrataḥ  /
viprāya vedaviduṣe tasya puṇyaṃ nibodhata  // 2,44.124 //
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvaiśvaryasamanvitaḥ  /
bhuktvā ca vipulānsvarge bhogāndivyānsuśobhanān  // 2,44.125 //
tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭo viprāṇāṃ jāyate kule  /
pūrvasaṃskāramāhātmyād brahmavidyāmavāpnuyāt  // 2,44.126 //
paṭhitvādhyāyamevaikaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  /
yor'thaṃ vicārayet samyak sa prāpnoti paraṃ padam  // 2,44.127 //
adhyetavyamidaṃ nityaṃ vipraiḥ parvaṇi parvaṇi  /
śrotavyaṃ ca dvijaśreṣṭhā mahāpātakanāśanam  // 2,44.128 //
ekatastu purāṇāni setihāsāni kṛtsnaśaḥ  /
ekatra cedaṃ paramametadevātiricyate  // 2,44.129 //
dharmanaipuṇyakāmānāṃ jñānanaipuṇyakāminām  /
idaṃ purāṇaṃ muktvaikaṃ nāstyanyat sādhanaṃ param  // 2,44.130 //
yathāvadatra bhagavān devo nārāyaṇo hariḥ  /
kathyate hi yathā viṣṇurna tathānyeṣu suvratāḥ  // 2,44.131 //
brāhmī paurāṇikī ceyaṃ saṃhitā pāpanāśanī  /
atra tat paramaṃ brahma kīrtyate hi yathārthataḥ  // 2,44.132 //
tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ tapasāṃ ca paraṃ tapaḥ  /
jñānānāṃ paramaṃ jñānaṃ vratānāṃ paramaṃ vratam  // 2,44.133 //
nādhyetavyamidaṃ śāstraṃ vṛṣalasya ca sannidhau  /
yo 'dhīte sa tu mohātmā sa yāti narakān bahūn  // 2,44.134 //
śrāddhe vā daivike kārye śrāvaṇīyaṃ dvijātibhiḥ  /
yajñānte tu viśeṣeṇa sarvadoṣaviśodhanam  // 2,44.135 //
mumukṣūṇāmidaṃ śāstramadhyetavyaṃ viśeṣataḥ  /
śrotavyaṃ cātha mantavyaṃ vedārthaparibṛṃhaṇam  // 2,44.136 //
jñātvā yathāvad viprendrān śrāvayed bhaktisaṃyutān  /
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmasāyujyamāpnuyāt  // 2,44.137 //
yo 'śraddadhāne puruṣe dadyāccādhārmike tathā  /
sa pretya gatvā nirayān śunāṃ yoniṃ vrajatyadhaḥ  // 2,44.138 //
namaskṛtvā hariṃ viṣṇuṃ jagadyoniṃ sanātanam  /
adhyetavyamidaṃ śāstraṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ tathā  // 2,44.139 //
ityājñā devadevasya viṣṇoramitatejasaḥ  /
pārāśaryasya viprarṣervyāsasya ca mahātmanaḥ  // 2,44.140 //
śrutvā nārāyaṇād divyāṃ nārado bhagavānṛṣiḥ  /
gautamāya dadau pūrvaṃ tasmāccaiva parāśaraḥ  // 2,44.141 //
parāśaro 'pi bhagavāna gaṅgādvāre munīśvarāḥ  /
munibhyaḥ kathayāmāsa dharmakāmārthamokṣadam  // 2,44.142 //
brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ sanakāya ca dhīmate  /
sanatkumārāya tathā sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  // 2,44.143 //
sanakād bhagavān sākṣād devalo yogavittamaḥ  /
avāptavān pañcaśikho devalādidamuttamam  // 2,44.144 //
sanatkumārād bhagavān muniḥ satyavatīsutaḥ  /
lebhe purāṇaṃ paramaṃ vyāsaḥ sarvārthasaṃcayam  // 2,44.145 //
tasmād vyāsādahaṃ śrutvā bhavatāṃ pāpanāśanam  /
ūcivān vai bhavadbhiśca dātavyaṃ dhārmike jane  // 2,44.146 //
tasmai vyāsāya gurave sarvajñāya maharṣaye  /
pārāśaryāya śāntāya namo nārāyaṇātmane  // 2,44.147 //
yasmāt saṃjāyate kṛtsanaṃ yatra caiva pralīyate  /
namastasmai sureśāya viṣṇave kūrmarūpiṇe  // 2,44.148 //

iti śrīkūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryāṃ saṃhitāyāmuparivibhāge catuścatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

uparivibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ


iti śrīkūrmapurāṇaṃ samāptam
